{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"Hyundai Malaysia officially teases ‘upcoming’ Kona","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166387","description":"<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/hyundai-malaysia-officially-teases-upcoming-kona/hyundai-malaysia-kona-fb-teaser/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166394\"><img src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Malaysia-Kona-FB-Teaser-630x709.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"709\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166394\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Malaysia-Kona-FB-Teaser-630x709.png 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Malaysia-Kona-FB-Teaser-850x957.png 850w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Malaysia-Kona-FB-Teaser.png 996w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>After some <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/19/spied-hyundai-kona-seen-in-malaysia-debut-soon/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">spyshots of the Hyundai Kona</a> were seen on the roads around Ara Damansara, where Hyundai-Sime Darby Motors (HSDM) is located, the brand&#8217;s Malaysian distributor has officially released a teaser post on its Facebook page. &#8220;A glance of the &#8216;upcoming&#8217; interior. You Drive it. You Define it,&#8221; the post reads.</p>\n<p>That upcoming interior belongs to the Kona, an easy spot thanks to the crossover&#8217;s body-coloured rings around the air con vents, gear lever and push start button. The pics below show the Kona in lime green and black; the former clearly displaying the two-tone body with black upper.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2018/11/22/klims18-hyundai-kona-electric-1-6-turbo-on-show-ice-version-set-for-q2-2019-malaysian-debut/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Previewed by HSDM</a> at the KL International Motor Show (KLIMS) 2018, the Kona was initially planned for a Q2 2019 introduction, but there have been some delays, and the unprecedented pandemic that hit the world this year certainly didn&#8217;t help to speed things up. But they appear to be ready now, and the Kona is just around the corner.</p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/19/spied-hyundai-kona-seen-in-malaysia-debut-soon/hyundai-kona-spied-in-malaysia-1/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Kona-spied-in-Malaysia-2-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Kona-spied-in-Malaysia-2-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Kona-spied-in-Malaysia-2-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Kona-spied-in-Malaysia-2-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Hyundai-Kona-spied-in-Malaysia-2-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p>Billed as the compact SUV for millennials, the Kona sits below the Hyundai Tucson and will attempt to tempt buyers away from the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/07/21/quick-look-2020-honda-hr-v-rs-brown-interior/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Honda HR-V</a>, <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/06/29/mazda-cx-3-limited-edition-accessories-package-bodykit-suede-interior-chassis-bracing-jbl-rm14-5k/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Mazda CX-3</a> and <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/03/01/gallery-2019-toyota-c-hr-new-wheels-carplay/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Toyota C-HR</a>. It certainly looks bold, with slit-like LED daytime running lights sitting separately above the main beams, which flank the corporate Cascading Grille. Fog lamps on a narrow lower intake make it three tiers of grilles and lights.</p>\n<p>The rear adopts the same tiered layout for the lamps. The Kona wears prominent &#8220;body armour&#8221; around the front and rear lamps, integrated with the wheel arches. It looks like nothing else on our roads and that&#8217;s a good thing.</p>\n<p>The Kona is 4,165 mm long and 1,800 mm wide; which makes it 129 mm shorter than a Honda HR-V, but 28 mm wider. Its roof is also 55 lower to the ground than the Honda, which gives the Korean a good stance. The wheelbase is 2,600 mm, which is just 10 mm short of the Honda, the sales and space champ of the B-SUV class.</p>\n\n<a and among them are a 2.0 litre MPI, 1.0 litre T-GDI three-cylinder and a 1.6 litre Gamma T-GDI. The latter – with 177 PS, 265 Nm of torque and a seven-speed dual-clutch automatic gearbox – was the one previewed at KLIMS. The turbo variant is good for 0-100 km/h in 7.9 seconds and a top speed of 205 km/h. There&#8217;s also a <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/07/20/hyundai-kona-electric-sales-crosses-100000-unit-mark/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Kona Electric full EV</a> version of the crossover. </p>\n<p>Available equipment from the global catalogue include a head-up display (HUD) with navigation, a premium sound system by Krell, wireless charging and Hyundai’s full suite of active safety and driver assist systems, as seen in our market&#8217;s Ioniq. </p>\n<p>Will the Kona be CKD locally assembled or CBU imported? Which engine will it carry? An attractively priced CKD with the T-GDI would be an interesting proposition next to its NA-powered Japanese rivals. _c5f0f8a4c76bb271.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-21-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn22@2020_5/2020/08/26/08-54-50-002_608daa85d95b8f80.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-22-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn41@2020_6/2020/08/26/08-54-57-373_0015ed81ce86c541.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-23-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn89@2020_5/2020/08/26/08-54-55-981_5151c735ca1a6d97.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-24-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn5@2020_4/2020/08/26/08-54-54-404_74f9066d2000603b.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-25-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn58@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-54-55-763_a69425acb4433119.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-26-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn25@2020_6/2020/08/26/08-54-51-675_ebf05545991fc3ad.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-27-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn38@2020_5/2020/08/26/08-54-50-012_bfebfb73e54d2bff.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-28-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn74@2020_3/2020/08/26/08-54-54-079_d62538e0b780a5f7.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-29-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn25@2020_4/2020/08/26/08-54-57-293_916d14c8d1d01652.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-30-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn49@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-54-53-930_cc869c3415d1c80b.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2018/11/KLIMS18_Hyundai_Kona-1.6-Turbo-32-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn70 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"2020 MINI John Cooper Works GP launched – hot two-seater F56 with 306 PS, just 10 units in M’sia, RM377k","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166300","description":"<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-launched-hot-two-seater-f56-with-306-ps-just-10-units-in-msia-rm377k/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-malaysia_ext-1/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166728\"><img src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-Malaysia_Ext-1-630x420.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" class=\"alignnone 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Aside from the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/\">MINI Cooper SE</a>, BMW Group Malaysia has also launched the new <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/11/20/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-3000-units-only/\">MINI John Cooper Works GP</a>. In stark contrast to its pure electric sibling, the GP takes Oxford&#8217;s internal combustion engine to the absolute zenith, becoming the hottest, most hardcore MINI you can buy.</p>\n<p>It&#8217;s also the most expensive MINI you can buy – it&#8217;s priced at RM388,888 on-the-road without insurance, and with the sales and service tax (SST) rebate, this figure drops to <strong>RM377,491</strong>. The GP is limited to 3,000 units worldwide and Malaysia gets an allocation of just ten.</p>\n<p>The secret to the GP&#8217;s <em>cili padi</em> performance lies under the bonnet. Here, you&#8217;ll find BMW&#8217;s most potent four-cylinder ever – an extensively-modified B48 2.0 litre turbocharged engine also found in the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/01/09/first-drive-2020-mini-john-cooper-works-clubman-and-countryman-malaysian-review-from-rm359k/\">JCW Clubman and Countryman</a>, along with <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/07/24/2020-f40-bmw-m135i-xdrive-launched-in-malaysia-amg-a35-rival-with-306-ps-450-nm-priced-at-rm356k/\">some BMW M Performance models</a>. It gets a reinforced crankshaft, new pistons, bushless connecting rods and a new torsional vibration damper with optimised cooling.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-launched-hot-two-seater-f56-with-306-ps-just-10-units-in-msia-rm377k/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-malaysia_ext-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166729\"><img src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-Malaysia_Ext-2-630x420.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166729\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-Malaysia_Ext-2-630x420.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-Malaysia_Ext-2-1200x800.jpg 1200w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-Malaysia_Ext-2-850x567.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>On top of that, there&#8217;s a new turbocharger with a blow-off valve, integrated into the exhaust manifold. The direct fuel injectors are also more precise and have an increased flow rate, while the larger oil sump has been reshaped. Last but not least, the cooling system gets twin coolant coolers, a bigger expansion tank, a unique coolant storage module and a more powerful electric fan to cope with the increased outputs. All in all, this engine kicks out 306 PS from 5,000 to 6,250 rpm and 450 Nm of torque from 1,750 to 4,500 rpm.</p>\n<p>Sadly for purists, you can no longer get the GP with a manual gearbox, the F56 version being only available with an eight-speed automatic transmission (incorporating a Torsen mechanical limited-slip differential). Still, the performance figures – which include a zero-to-100 km/h sprint time of 5.2 seconds and an unrestrained top speed of 265 km/h – should be enough recompense. A specially-designed exhaust system, fitted with twin brushed stainless steel tailpipes, adds some aural drama.</p>\n<p>That&#8217;s just the start – to save weight, the GP, just like its predecessors, is only available as a two-seater. It also comes with a whole host of chassis tweaks, such as stiffer engine mounts, a front strut tower brace and a massive rear brace that takes the place of the rear seats.</p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-launched-hot-two-seater-f56-with-306-ps-just-10-units-in-msia-rm377k/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-malaysia_int-1/'><img 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p>Going hand-in-hand with the increased body rigidity is the retuned suspension. For a start, the track widths have been increased for the first time on the GP, necessitating the fitment of wider fenders to clear the 18-inch forged alloy wheels. Those alloys weigh less than nine kilograms apiece and come in a distinctive eight-spoke design, shod with 225/35 R18 tyres.</p>\n<p>The car also rides 10 mm lower than standard and gets revised springs, auxiliary springs, dampers and anti-roll bars, and increased negative camber. Elsewhere, there are preloaded anti-roll bar bushings, stiffer rubber bearings and boll-jointed rear wishbones, along with upgraded brakes with four-piston front callipers and 380 mm front discs. The stability control system also has a GP mode with more lenient intervention.</p>\n<p>Setting the GP apart from lesser models visually are the aggressive aerodynamics, consisting of a unique front air dam design, a larger front splitter, a beefier rear diffuser and a massive bi-plane rear wing. The boxy wheel arch extensions are made of carbon fibre and not only hide the wider track but also optimise the flow of air. The numbering of the limited series is applied to the front wings using a new paint transfer process.</p>\n<p>\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-john-cooper-works-gp-launched-hot-two-seater-f56-with-306-ps-just-10-units-in-msia-rm377k/mini_jcw_gp_specsheet_pm/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-spec-sheet-2-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-spec-sheet-2-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/MINI-John-Cooper-Works-GP-spec-sheet-2-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<center><em>Click to enlarge</em></center></p>\n<p>Inside, you&#8217;ll find JCW sports seats with integrated headrests, stainless steel pedals and a unique three-spoke steering wheel with a 3D-printed metal 12 o&#8217;clock marker and perforated paddle shifters. The passenger-side trim panel, which bears the serial number, is also 3D-printed, while the instrument cluster is a 6.5-inch digital display much like the Cooper SE, with unique graphics and displays.</p>\n<p>Just one colour combination is available for the GP – Racing Grey with a Melting Silver roof and door mirrors, gloss black exterior trim and red side stripes and highlights. Inside, you&#8217;ll find leather and Dinamica microfibre upholstery, red GP logos and the gloss red rear brace.</p>\n<p>Standard equipment includes LED headlights, Union Jack LED tail lights, toggle-switch start (no keyless entry, unfortunately), cruise control, dual-zone automatic climate control, the MINI Visual Boost navigation system with an 8.8-inch touchscreen, Apple CarPlay compatibility and Qi wireless smartphone charging. Safety-wise, there are six airbags and stability control; unfortunately, unlike the Cooper SE, the GP does not come with autonomous emergency braking, but we understand that this is the case globally as well.</p>\n\n<a 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"Koenigsegg Gemera – CEO gives a video walkthrough","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166926","description":"<p><iframe width=\"630\" height=\"354\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/hGg5tatQEY0?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen></iframe></p>\n<p>So, you’ve already laid your eyes on the rather exciting <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/03/04/koenigsegg-gemera-four-seater-with-2l-3-cylinder-freevalve-engine-three-electric-motors/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Koenigsegg Gemera</a>, but there’s just one problem: is it really that spacious? Sure, the performance figures are amazing, but can the sporty, two-door, four-seater actually accommodate grown adults? Well, wonder no more, as the boss of the Swedish carmaker, Christian von Koenigsegg, is here to demonstrate just that.</p>\n<p>In a walkthrough video posted on Koenigsegg’s official YouTube page, we’re introduced to four random men of varying heights, from as “short” as 196 cm to a towering 202 cm. These individuals then proceed to climb into the Gemera, and they appear to be seated in relative comfort, so there’s your answer.</p>\n<p>The demonstration also showcased one of the Gemera’s party tricks, and that is its Autoskin electro-hydraulic system. This first appear on the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2015/11/17/video-koenigsegg-regera-autoskin-auto-doors/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Regera</a>, and allows one to open the bonnets and doors of the car with just a push of a button on the key fob, which is great for showing off.</p>\n<p>Of course, the video doesn’t stop there, as Christian then proceeds to talk a bit about his company’s latest creation, which was inspired by the Lotus Excel SE built from 1982 to 1992. Like the Gemera, the classic Lotus model was a two-door coupe that offered 2+2 seating, which Christian had fond childhood memories in.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/koenigsegg-gemera-ceo-gives-a-video-walkthrough/koenigsegg-gemera-walkthrough-1/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166958\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-1-630x330.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"330\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166958\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-1-630x330.jpg 630w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-1-1200x628.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-1-850x445.jpg 850w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-1.jpg 1425w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The idea for the Gemera was conceptualised by the Koenigsegg boss almost 15 years ago, but at the time, he lacked access to the development tools and technologies to make that dream a reality. Of course, he did make it work in the end, because here we have a mid-engined sports car that can fit four, two-metre adults and four carry-on luggage sets – as you’ll see in the video -with ease, something unheard of in this form factor.</p>\n<p>If that isn’t impress enough, the Gemera isn’t exactly barren on the inside either, as there are eight cupholders – half of them heated while the remaining four are cooled – as well as a rear-seat entertainment system. </p>\n<p>For some fun trivia, the seats feature memory foam that was pioneered by the CC8S nearly 20 years ago, and the ones at the front are made from carbon-fibre with integrated seatbelts. Thankfully the seats’ hollow monocoque is manufactured using the same Aircore technology as the wheels, making them incredibly light: each one weighs under 20 kg. </p>\n<p>We can’t talk about the Gemera without mentioning its powertrain, which at its core is the Tiny Friendly Giant (TFG) engine. The 2.0 litre unit that features the company’s Freevalve camless technology, two turbochargers, dry sump lubrication, flex fuel-capability, an 8,500 rpm redline and weighs just 70 kg.</p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/koenigsegg-gemera-ceo-gives-a-video-walkthrough/koenigsegg-gemera-walkthrough-2/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-2-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-2-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-2-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-2-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-2-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-2-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/koenigsegg-gemera-ceo-gives-a-video-walkthrough/koenigsegg-gemera-walkthrough-3/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-3-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-3-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-3-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-3-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-3-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Koenigsegg-Gemera-walkthrough-3-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p>On its own, the TFG makes 600 PS (590 hp) at 7,500 rpm, while peak torque is 600 Nm from 2,000 to 7,000 rpm. This is mounted midship, with drive going to the front wheels via Koenigsegg’s Direct Drive (KDD) transmission and a propshaft. The single-gear KDD features the company’s HydraCoup (hydraulic coupling) technology for a direct link from the engine to the front axle, and is paired with an electric motor that is rated at 400 PS (395 hp) and 500 Nm.</p>\n<p>Adding to these bits are a pair of electric motors at the rear – one wheel apiece &#8211; with each one providing 500 PS (493 hp) and 1,000 Nm. All in, the Gemera has a total output of 1,700 PS (1,677 hp or 1.27 MW) and 3,500 Nm of torque, or 1,100 PS (1,085 hp) when only the electric motors are at work, drawing power from an 800-volt, 16.6-kWh battery mounted under the front seats.</p>\n<p>Performance-wise, the Koenigsegg family car will get from zero to 100 km/h time in just 1.9 seconds, while a sprint from a dead stop to 400 km/h comes at a “record matching pace,” the company says. On electric power alone, the battery provides a range of up to 50 km, while with just the internal combustion engine, it goes up to 950 km – the total range is 1,000 km.</p>\n<p>Unfortunately, only 300 units of the Gemera will be built for the entire world, so it’s very unlikely we’ll get to see one in person, or even own one given the high price tag that is said to be in the region of 1.7 million euros (RM8.38 million). However, if you do, it’s quite an engineering feat to behold, don’t you think?</p>\n<p><strong>GALLERY: Koenigsegg Gemera</strong>\n<a 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"BMW iX – production iNEXT to come in three versions","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166560","description":"<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/02/28/bmw-inext-electric-suv-new-photos-show-more-skin/bmw-inext-hot-weather-7/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1088579\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/02/BMW-iNEXT-hot-weather-7-e1582857564959-630x356.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"356\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1088579\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/02/BMW-iNEXT-hot-weather-7-e1582857564959-630x356.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/02/BMW-iNEXT-hot-weather-7-e1582857564959-1200x677.jpg 1200w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/02/BMW-iNEXT-hot-weather-7-e1582857564959-210x120.jpg 210w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/02/BMW-iNEXT-hot-weather-7-e1582857564959-850x480.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The upcoming, production version of the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/02/28/bmw-inext-electric-suv-new-photos-show-more-skin/\">BMW iNEXT</a>, to be called the iX, will be available in three versions, <a href=\"https://www.bmwblog.com/2020/08/11/bmw-ix-inext-will-come-in-three-flavors-from-300-to-600-hp/\"><em>BMW Blog</em></a> reports. These will start from 308 hp in entry level guise, through a mid-range 522 hp model, up to 610 hp in its most powerful form. </p>\n<p>In terms of comparable internal combustion outputs, the X5 xDrive40i produces 340 PS and 450 Nm of torque, while a <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/12/10/2020-bmw-x3-x4-m40i-m550i-get-huge-power-bump-for-the-us-m550is-4-4l-v8-makes-523-hp-750-nm/\">&#8217;50i&#8217; powertrain</a> produces 523 hp and 750 Nm of torque. The top performance variant would be comparable to the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/10/02/f95-bmw-x5-m-and-f96-x6-m-debut-with-competition-versions/\">X5 M</a>, which outputs 617 hp and 750 Nm.  </p>\n<p>The BMW iX will reportedly also feature an innovation called BMW Natural Interaction, according to the report, which is based on the &#8216;Shy Tech&#8217; touch operation concept that first emerged on the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2018/09/19/bmw-vision-inext-previews-all-electric-suv-for-2021/\">Vision iNEXT concept vehicle</a>. </p>\n<p>This will employ materials that enable virtually any interior surface to serve as a control display, and stay hidden until its touch functions are needed. According to <em>BMW Blog</em>, this technology will be introduced on the production iX as well as future high-end BMWs. </p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/05/13/spyshots-bmw-inext-spotted-interior-revealed/bmw-inext-spyshots-9/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-958898\"><img src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/05/BMW-iNEXT-spyshots-9-630x397.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"397\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-958898\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/05/BMW-iNEXT-spyshots-9-630x397.jpg 630w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/05/BMW-iNEXT-spyshots-9-1200x756.jpg 1200w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/05/BMW-iNEXT-spyshots-9-850x536.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p><center><em>BMW iNEXT <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/05/13/spyshots-bmw-inext-spotted-interior-revealed/\">spied during testing</a></em></center></p>\n<p>Naturally, the iX will be all-wheel-drive, and it will be a model sized between the X3 and the X5. An earlier report by <a href=\"https://www.autoexpress.co.uk/bmw/104621/new-2021-bmw-inext-targets-360-mile-range\"><em>Auto Express</em></a> suggested that the fully electric SUV will have battery range up to 580 km, and this is likely to be supplied by a battery pack of around 100 kWh in capacity. Optional equipment on the iX can be expected to the on par with that of the 5 Series, which includes air suspension and soft-close doors. Wheel sizes on the iX will be from 20 inches to 22 inches in diameter, the report said. </p>\n<p>So far, we know that the interior of the iX will feature a <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/07/22/bmw-inext-flat-bottomed-steering-wheel-revealed/\">two-spoke &#8216;polygonal&#8217; steering wheel</a>, a shape that was chosen to be more suited to autonomous driving, BMW said previously. The iX could feature autonomous driving at levels of up to <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/07/10/autonomous-driving-tech-level-0-to-level-5-explained/\">Level 3</a>, according to earlier reports. </p>\n<p>This is because the shape will help the driver more easily recognise the angle of the steering wheel when switching back to manual driving, and be safer as a result. the flat top and bottom of the wheel rim also aids entry and egress, as well as giving the driver more room to bend their legs for comfort when using the adaptive cruise control.</p>\n<p>The BMW iX is set to make its debut soon, however production will only commence in July next year, <em>BMW Blog</em> reported. Customer deliveries for overseas markets will be staggered, and the United States is estimated to receive the first customer units in 2022. </p>\n<p><strong>GALLERY: BMW iNEXT, hot weather for the 2021 model year, after the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/19/2021-mazda-cx-9-launched-in-the-us-three-row-suv-gets-10-25-inch-display-new-carbon-edition-trim-level/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">CX-9</a> just a few days ago. Set to arrive in dealerships next month, the SUV retails from USD25,270 (RM105,310) up to USD37,405 (RM155,882), with seven trim levels to choose from.</p>\n<p>From the seven options, the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/14/mazda-6-cx-5-cx-9-receive-carbon-edition-variants/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Carbon Edition</a> and Carbon Edition Turbo are new additions and feature exclusive styling elements like a Polymetal Grey exterior finish, gloss black door mirrors and 19-inch black metallic aluminium alloy wheels. Both also get red leather seats and black honeycomb interior trim on the dashboard and door panels, along with red stitching on the steering wheel and shift knob.</p>\n<p>On the Carbon Edition, power comes from a SkyActiv-G 2.5 litre naturally-aspirated four-cylinder petrol engine that makes 187 hp and 252 Nm of torque. Meanwhile, the Turbo version adds on a turbocharger for 250 hp and 434 Nm with premium 93 octane fuel, or 227 hp and 420 Nm with regular 87 octane fuel.</p>\n<p>The non-turbo engine is also used for the base Sport, Touring and Grand Touring, while the Grand Touring Reserve and Signature come with the turbo mill instead. A six-speed automatic transmission, G-Vectoring Control Plus (GVC Plus) and front-wheel drive are standard from the Sport to the Grand Touring, with the option of all-wheel drive, but only the upper two trims come exclusively with AWD.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2021-mazda-cx-5-debuts-in-the-us-carbon-edition-models-added-new-10-25-inch-infotainment-display/2021-mazda-cx-5-us-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166517\"><img src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Mazda-CX-5-US-2-630x420.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"420\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166517\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Mazda-CX-5-US-2-630x420.jpg 630w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Mazda-CX-5-US-2-1200x800.jpg 1200w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Mazda-CX-5-US-2-850x567.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>In terms of equipment changes, all CX-5 trims come with a new 10.25-inch infotainment display that has support for Android Auto, Apple CarPlay and other connected services. Also standard is the i-Activsense suite, which includes Mazda Radar Cruise Control with stop and go function, Advanced Smart City Brake Support with pedestrian detection, Smart Brake Support, Lane Departure Warning with Lane-Keep Assist and Blind Spot Monitoring with Rear Cross-Traffic Alert.</p>\n<p>The Touring trim now gets more goodies for rear passengers, including air vents and a centre armrest with two USB charging ports. It also gains the Mazda Advanced Keyless Entry system, rear privacy glass, a six-speaker sound system and auto-levelling function for the LED headlamps. An optional Touring Preferred SV package adds on a 10-speaker Bose sound system, leather seats, a powered liftgate, a powered sunroof, an auto-dimming rear-view mirror and powered front seats.</p>\n<p>On the Grand Touring, enhancements include items found on the Touring with the optional package, along with a seven-inch digital instrument cluster. Meanwhile, the Grand Touring Reserve gains a windshield-projected head-up display, ventilated front seats, heated rear seats and steering wheel, automatic folding door mirrors and a windshield wiper de-icer.</p>\n<p>Lastly, the range-topping Signature’s i-Activsense suite gains Smart City Brake Support Reverse and Driver Attention Alert, which join the around-view monitor with front and rear parking sensors. The kit list also includes Caturra Brown Nappa leather seats, genuine layered wood trimming, frameless, ambient LED interior lighting, 19-inch dark silver aluminum alloy wheels, a black headliner and href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/rolls-royce-unveils-new-brand-identity-purple-spirit-signature-colour-now-calls-itself-a-house-of-luxury/rolls-royce-rebranding-2020-1/\" rel=\"attachment modern, and more in tune with both the digital world and its now younger client demographic. Also, the Goodwood carmaker is now calling itself a &#8220;House of Luxury&#8221; instead of just an automotive manufacturer.</p>\n<p>According to Rolls-Royce, it has of late experienced change at a quicker rate than ever before. The brand&#8217;s portfolio has expanded to five models, and almost every car created is bespoke. The introduction of <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/06/30/rolls-royce-black-badge-family-launched-in-malaysia-ghost-wraith-dawn-cullinan-on-sale-fr-rm1-4-mil/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Black Badge</a> has answered the call for an edgier, alternative R-R, &#8220;one that carries an assertive and dominant persona,&#8221; Rolls-Royce says, adding that the age of its clients have decreased to an average of just 43.</p>\n<p>&#8220;As the marque&#8217;s digital presence increases, there has never been a more important time for the visual language of the company to reflect our standing as the leading luxury brand in the world. We have embarked on a fascinating journey of modernising our brand identity to echo those changes seen in our portfolio, our client demographic, their lifestyle and the luxury world that surrounds them,&#8221; Rolls-Royce CEO Torsten Muller-Otvos explained. </p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/06/30/rolls-royce-black-badge-family-launched-in-malaysia-ghost-wraith-dawn-cullinan-on-sale-fr-rm1-4-mil/2020-rolls-royce-black-badge-family-in-malaysia-8/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1138430\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/06/2020-Rolls-Royce-Black-Badge-Family-in-Malaysia-8-630x330.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"330\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1138430\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/06/2020-Rolls-Royce-Black-Badge-Family-in-Malaysia-8-630x330.jpg 630w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/06/2020-Rolls-Royce-Black-Badge-Family-in-Malaysia-8-1200x628.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/06/2020-Rolls-Royce-Black-Badge-Family-in-Malaysia-8-850x445.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Rolls-Royce appointed Marina Willer, partner at multi-disciplinary design studio Pentagram, to create a new brand identity that encapsulates the brand’s presence and standing as a House of Luxury. The identity was designed to appeal to the new demographic of clients and all that they represent, digitally and physically.</p>\n<p>Pentagram embarked upon a deep dive into Rolls-Royce, including its products (both new and old), design ethos, designers, items that are sacrosanct to the marque, and the unique relationship Goodwood maintains with its clients. They also spent time in the factory, understanding <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/13/rolls-royce-wraith-eagle-viii-le-marks-first-non-stop-transatlantic-flight-1-of-50-sold-for-rm3-3m-in-malaysia/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">the essence of bespoke</a>.</p>\n<p>&#8220;What soon became apparent is that Rolls-Royce has evolved from being regarded as an automotive manufacturer into a leading light in the world of luxury. It was essential for us to ensure that the brand&#8217;s new identity reflected this shift. We needed to present Rolls-Royce in a forward-facing, fresh and relevant way &#8211; speaking to new audiences while respecting the company’s loyal clients,&#8221; Willer commented.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/rolls-royce-unveils-new-brand-identity-purple-spirit-signature-colour-now-calls-itself-a-house-of-luxury/rolls-royce-rebranding-2020-4/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166707\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-4-630x354.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"354\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166707\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-4-630x354.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-4-1200x675.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-4-850x478.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>She was able to approach the redesign from a fresh perspective. &#8220;I do not come from an automotive background. This vantage point provided me with the opportunity to observe Rolls-Royce as a manufacturer of luxury products. My ambition was to celebrate the luxuriousness of the brand while providing it with the means to visually communicate with Rolls-Royce’s younger, increasingly diversified audiences,&#8221; she said.</p>\n<p>Let&#8217;s start with the brand&#8217;s iconic Spirit of Ecstasy sculpture. Having graced the prow of Rolls-Royce cars since 1911, she will remain unchanged, but the Spirit of Ecstasy will now gain increased prominence in the marque&#8217;s brand identity. This will be done via an illustration, a distilled form of the statuette. When depicted in 2D form, her direction is from left to right, &#8220;boldly facing the future&#8221;.</p>\n<p>You would have noticed the deep purple backgrounds here, and the colour was chosen out of a desire to seek a more expressive, luxurious colour palette, one appealing to both male and female clients. &#8220;Historically rare in nature and with roots in mythology, art, piety and royalty, purple has always signified wealth and power,&#8221; R-R says, and with that, Purple Spirit will be its signature colour. A metallic rose gold was chosen to complement the purple, but only on printed material.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/rolls-royce-unveils-new-brand-identity-purple-spirit-signature-colour-now-calls-itself-a-house-of-luxury/rolls-royce-rebranding-2020-3/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166706\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-3-630x354.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"354\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166706\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-3-630x354.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-3-850x478.jpg 850w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-3.jpg 960w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The double R &#8220;Badge of Honour&#8221; remains unchanged, but from now, is reserved solely for the creations of the Home of Rolls-Royce in Goodwood, which has to be the cars. The monogram &#8211; just the double R without the Rolls-Royce wording &#8211; also retains its original form but replaces the Badge of Honour on collateral.</p>\n<p>However, the wordmark &#8216;Rolls-Royce Motor Cars&#8217;, as found above the door of the marque&#8217;s establishments, was found to be corporate and unrepresentative of the House of Luxury the brand wants to be. Pentagram uncovered typography in the marque&#8217;s archives from the 1930s and used an art-deco style as the basis of a new wordmark. The words &#8216;Motor Cars&#8217; have reduced in size, with the emphasis reverting to Rolls-Royce. Note that the two Rs are ever slightly more prominent.</p>\n<p>Pentagram’s design team explored multiple typefaces in search of a font that depicts luxury, without being overtly decorative. The chosen typeface, Riviera Nights, stems from the same family as Gill Sans Alt, the marque&#8217;s previous font, but with additionally crafted and bevelled letters.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/rolls-royce-unveils-new-brand-identity-purple-spirit-signature-colour-now-calls-itself-a-house-of-luxury/rolls-royce-rebranding-2020-5/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166709\"><img src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-5-630x354.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"354\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166709\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-5-630x354.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-5-1200x675.jpg 1200w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/Rolls-Royce-Rebranding-2020-5-850x478.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Lastly, to tie all the above together is a new visual treatment of the Spirit of Ecstasy, called The Spirit of Ecstasy Expression. Akin to silken fabric, The Expression adopts a fluid form and is versatile in nature, adding a &#8220;cutting-edge aura&#8221; to the new visual identity. A digital tool that uses coding has been developed by Pentagram to enable The Expression to be used on any surface, from projection to embroidery, printing to engraving. It will be found in both physical (at showrooms) and digital forms.</p>\n<p>There you go, different logos for different items, all connected in one new brand identity. If all of the above doesn&#8217;t make much sense to you, at least you&#8217;ll agree that the new visuals look both modern and luxurious. </p>\n<p>\n<a /08/26/08-54-56-485_73908ad9985c641b.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Rolls-Royce-Cullinan-Black-Badge-Malaysia_Int-34-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn21@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-54-54-525_d82c42363d75b648.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Rolls-Royce-Cullinan-Black-Badge-Malaysia_Int-35-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn81@2020_1/2020/08/26/08-54-56-755_f627722f2c3c7988.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Rolls-Royce-Cullinan-Black-Badge-Malaysia_Int-36-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn13@2020_5/2020/08/26/08-54-51-154_58140885003c323f.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Rolls-Royce-Cullinan-Black-Badge-Malaysia_Int-37-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn89@2020_4/2020/08/26/08-54-50-472_40f37d6dea06c52e.webp","http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Rolls-Royce-Cullinan-Black-Badge-Malaysia_Int-38-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn42@2020_6/2020/08/26/08-54-53-911_d961cfbc92ef48d9.webp","http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Rolls-Royce-Cullinan-Black-Badge-Malaysia_Int-39-108x108.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn18@2020_3/2020/08/26/08-54-56-383_69dbd9e3589c4bd2.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598432082973},{"createdTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"2020 MINI Cooper SE launched in Malaysia – electric vehicle with 184 PS, 270 Nm, 234 km range, RM218,380","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166281","description":"<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/mini-cooper-se-1/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166565\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/MINI-Cooper-SE-1-630x330.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"330\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166565\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/MINI-Cooper-SE-1-630x330.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/MINI-Cooper-SE-1.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/MINI-Cooper-SE-1-850x445.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>After dropping <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/02/04/g20-bmw-330e-mini-cooper-se-coming-to-msia-2020/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">hints</a> and <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/06/12/2020-mini-cooper-se-teased-before-malaysian-launch/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">teasers</a> throughout the year, BMW Group Malaysia has finally launched the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/02/03/2020-mini-cooper-se-more-technical-details-revealed/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">fully electric MINI Cooper SE</a>. It broke cover just <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/07/10/mini-cooper-se-makes-its-official-debut/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">a little over a year ago</a>, and there&#8217;s just one configuration on offer here. It&#8217;s fully imported from the UK and is priced at a cool <strong>RM218,380</strong> (after <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/06/12/2020-sst-exemption-mini-malaysia-releases-new-prices-up-to-rm13997-cheaper-until-december-31/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">SST exemption</a>; otherwise it&#8217;s <strong>RM225,888</strong>). The equipment list, as you&#8217;ll find out, is actually pretty impressive considering the price.</p>\n<p>Included in the price is a four-year unlimited mileage warranty with free scheduled service, as well as an eight-year or 100,000 km warranty for the high voltage battery. Just to compare, the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/02/18/mini-cooper-se-now-in-thailand-ev-goes-for-rm304k/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Cooper SE in Thailand is priced at RM304k</a>.</p>\n<p>The Cooper SE shares the same UKL platform as the regular <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2018/07/13/mini-hatch-facelift-launched-in-malaysia-cooper-s-3-door-and-5-door-jcw-3-door-rm227k-to-rm283k/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">3 Door and 5 Door hatches</a>, so dimensions, design proportions, and interior space are more or less identical. Its electric propulsion unit is rather familiar, actually, one derived from the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/08/02/bmw-i3s-ev-official-pricing-revealed-rm278800-otr/\">BMW i3s</a>.</p>\n<p>The compact electric motor (which weighs less than a conventional engine) provides 184 hp (135 kW) at 7,000 rpm and 270 Nm of torque from 100 to 1,000 rpm. Comparatively, the regular Cooper S’ offers 192 hp and 280 Nm of torque from its B48 2.0 litre engine.</p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/2020-mini-cooper-se-malaysia_ext-2/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-2-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-2-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-2-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-2-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-2-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-2-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/2020-mini-cooper-se-malaysia_ext-27/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-27-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-27-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-27-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-27-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-27-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Ext-27-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p>Being a city car, the Cooper SE is tuned specifically to provide peak acceleration at up to 60 km/h. As such, the 0-60 km/h sprint is done in 3.9 seconds, but the century sprint is achieved in 7.3 seconds. A single-stage transmission is standard, and note that the top speed is electronically limited to 150 km/h.</p>\n<p>Under the floor rests a new, specially-developed T-shaped 32.6 kWh lithium-ion battery pack with a net content of 28.9 kWh and operates at 350.4 volts. MINI says this is good for a driving range of up to 234 km (WLTP cycle; 270 km on NEDC cycle).</p>\n<p>For charging, the car comes with an 11 kW onboard charger and a Type 2 to 3-pin household plug charging cable (dubbed the contingency cable) as standard. Of course, owners are recommended to get the optional 22 kW MINI Wallbox Plus (with an integrated Type 2 cable), available for RM6,500. An additional five-metre, Type 2 three-phase cable for use with public chargers goes for RM1,388.20.</p>\n<p>Charging the car from 0-80% takes 12 hours with the contingency cable (3-pin household plug). With an 11 kW three-phase wallbox, it takes 3.5 hours to fully charge the car (2.5 hours from 0-80%), or 4.2 hours through a 7.4 kW single-phase wallbox. It also supports up to 50 kW DC fast-charging, taking just 1.4 hours for a full charge (36 minutes from 0-80%), but this requires a CCS Combo 2 connection.</p>\n<p>\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/2020-mini-cooper-se-spec-sheet/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Spec-Sheet-e1598415549300-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Spec-Sheet-e1598415549300-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Spec-Sheet-e1598415549300-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Spec-Sheet-e1598415549300-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Spec-Sheet-e1598415549300-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Spec-Sheet-e1598415549300-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<a http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE_2-e1598415499918-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE_2-e1598415499918-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE_2-e1598415499918-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<br />\n<center><em>Click to enlarge</em></center></p>\n<p>To provide protection for the battery, the car&#8217;s height is raised by 18 mm, and a solid base plate protects it from road debris. In the event of an accident, an automatic failsafe function immediately switches off all drive components. With all these, the Cooper SE weighs just 145 kg more than the Cooper S 3 Door. Not bad.</p>\n<p>Other unique features include two levels of brake regeneration (-0.19 m/s/s and -0.11 m/s/s), single-joint McPherson strut with aluminium swivel bearing up front, rear multi-link setup, with weight-optimised trailing arms. No adaptive dampers or sports suspension here.</p>\n<p>Design-wise, the EV is pretty distinctive, featuring psychedelic yellow highlights on the closed radiator grille, side mirror caps, scuttle plates, alloy wheels, and tailgate decors. We get the larger 17-inch <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/04/23/mini-cooper-se-corona-spoke-wheels-renamed/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">Power Spoke wheels</a> (previously called Corona Spoke) that&#8217;s unique only to the Cooper SE. Matrix LED headlights and tail lights with the Union Jack motif are standard. Three colours are available &#8211; Chili Red, British Racing Green, and White Silver, which you see here. </p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/2020-mini-cooper-se-malaysia_int-1/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-1-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-1-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-1-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-1-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-1-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-1-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/2020-mini-cooper-se-malaysia_int-4/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-4-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-4-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-4-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-4-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-4-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-MINI-Cooper-SE-Malaysia_Int-4-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p>Inside, you get the familiar MINI Hatch cabin, except the driver gets a brand new 5.5-inch digital instrument display with the same yellow theme. There&#8217;s also a yellow start-stop ignition toggle instead of red, eDrive mode (Sport, Mid, Green, and Green+), dual-zone climate control, 12-colour ambient lighting system, and the range-topping 8.8-inch touchscreen MINI Visual Boost with MINI Connected.</p>\n<p>Also on are head-up display, 12-speaker Harman Kardon Sound System, a wireless charging tray in the centre armrest, Carbon Black interior appointments, anthracite headliner, and leather seats with cross punch upholstery. Boot space remains unimpeded with 211 litres (same as the regular 3 Door), and can be expanded to 731 litres.</p>\n<p>Lastly, for safety, the Cooper SE gets the Driving Assistant and Parking Assistant packs as standard, which includes functions such as autonomous emergency braking (Light City Braking Function; between 6 km/h to 60 km/h), Traffic Sign Recognition, as well as Approach Control Warning and Person Warning.</p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-mini-cooper-se-launched-in-malaysia-rm218k/2020-mini-cooper-se-malaysia_ext-1/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"2020 Triumph Trident design prototype revealed","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166391","description":"<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-triumph-trident-design-prototype-revealed/2020-triumph-trident-design-prototype-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166461\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-2-e1598411726395-630x417.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"417\" class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-1166461\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-2-e1598411726395-630x417.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-2-e1598411726395.jpg 729w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Indicating plans to move into the small displacement market are moving ahead, the covers have been taken off the Triumph Trident design prototype. The design mock-up, finished in white, shows off the general proportions and lines of the upcoming model, with which Triumph intends to enter the middleweight commuter/light sports motorcycle market.</p>\n<p>Not as edgy as the more sports oriented 765, nor a throwback to the classic design of the Street Twin, the Trident falls somewhere in the middle ground of an all-rounder motorcycle. Meant to sit in the Triumph catalogue under the 765, it is clear Triumph intends to compete with market offerings such as the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2018/02/01/review-2017-kawasaki-ninja-650-and-z650-malaysia/\">Kawasaki Z650</a>, <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2016/09/20/review-2016-yamaha-mt-07-mid-size-wheelie-madness/\">Yamaha MT-07</a> and <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/01/17/review-2019-honda-cbr650r-and-cb650r-inline-four-middleweights-for-every-rider-from-rm43999/\">Honda CB650R</a>.</p>\n<p>In theory, this would place the Trident&#8217;s market price around the RM45,000 mark, suitable for the budget-conscious rider who needs a machine a step above a 250. Perusing the press photographs, the Trident&#8217;s design has been kept simple with a new frame made from steel tube and welded stampings wrapped around the Triumph Triple.</p>\n\n<a http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-4-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-4-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-4-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p>This also applies to the asymmetrical gullwing swing arm which seems to be a welded pressed unit &#8211; cheaper and easier to manufacture &#8211; rather than the cast alloy unit on the 765. The engine is also not a downsized unit from the 765 as although there is a resemblance in the head, the engine casing are short and different in design.</p>\n<p>The design prototype also shows upside-down forks and we will assume these might be non-adjustable units due to cost considerations. Nissan brake callipers are also shown, with what looks like two-piston units in front and a single-piston calliper at the back.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-triumph-trident-design-prototype-revealed/2020-triumph-trident-design-prototype-3/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166462\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776-630x447.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"447\" class=\"aligncenter size-medium wp-image-1166462\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776-630x447.jpg 630w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776-1200x851.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776-135x96.jpg 135w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776-161x115.jpg 161w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776-210x150.jpg 210w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776-850x603.jpg 850w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2020-Triumph-Trident-Design-Prototype-3-e1598411904776.jpg 1305w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Up top, the twin headlamp design from the 765 has been replaced with a single round LED headlight and inside the cockpit a single round LED display keeps things simple and a little retro looking. The fuel tank looks to be massive, with design lines throwing back to the original Triumph Trident from the 1970s.</p>\n<p>There was little other information released, such as displacement or power figures but for this market segment, the norm seems to be around 60 to 70 horsepower. Triumph has stated the Trident will come in a detuned version for new license holders which can then be retuned to provide full power once the rider passes his or her license restriction.</p>\n<p><iframe width=\"630\" height=\"354\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/4AIN_zfEmbU?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen></iframe><br />\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2020-triumph-trident-design-prototype-revealed/2020-triumph-trident-design-prototype-1/'><img 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"2021 Hyundai Kona facelift teased, with N Line variant","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166368","description":"<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2021-hyundai-kona-facelift-teased-with-n-line-variant/2021-hyundai-kona-teaser-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-1166372\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-2-e1598408285897-630x330.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"330\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-1166372\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-2-e1598408285897-630x330.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-2-e1598408285897-1200x629.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-2-e1598408285897-850x445.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Hyundai has released a set of teaser images for the facelifted iteration of its compact SUV, the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2017/06/13/hyundai-kona-compact-suv-for-millennials-revealed/\">Kona</a> along with an accompanying N Line variant &#8211; a full-on performance <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/07/22/spied-hyundai-kona-n-spotted-at-the-nurburgring/\">Kona N</a> is in the works &#8211; where the images partially show the car&#8217;s front end that has been redesigned to gain more visual width. This is the latest application of the brand&#8217;s Sensuous Sportiness design identity, the carmaker said.</p>\n<p>The facelifted Kona wears a &#8216;shark-inspired nose&#8217; that aids in adding said visual width, while the main headlamps  are now a trio of three-dimensional elements on each side, replacing the current model&#8217;s round lights framed within trim surrounds at each front corner. The new grille design is comprise of larger pins, which are now also more three-dimensional.</p>\n<p>The fascia has been further cleaned up with the removal of the inboard foglamps that were within the lower intake, which is now larger and slightly closer in size to the main grille on the N Line variant. At the upper end, the slim daytime running lights remain albeit with redesigned internal elements. </p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2021-hyundai-kona-facelift-teased-with-n-line-variant/2021-hyundai-kona-teaser-1/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-1-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-1-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-1-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-1-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-1-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-1-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2020/08/26/2021-hyundai-kona-facelift-teased-with-n-line-variant/2021-hyundai-kona-teaser-3/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-3-e1598408621929-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-3-e1598408621929-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-3-e1598408621929-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-3-e1598408621929-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-3-e1598408621929-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2020/08/2021-Hyundai-Kona-teaser-3-e1598408621929-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p><center><em>N Line version (left) offers a style variation. Click to enlarge</em></center></p>\n<p>Meanwhile, the central letterbox intake of the current model has been resculpted into a trio of smaller inlets between the DRLs on the N Line and relocates the brand logo to the centre of the main grille, while the standard style does without the top intakes. Along the lower corners of the bumper, the N Line variant gets an additional horizontal element below each main lamp. </p>\n<p>In Malaysia, the Kona has been <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/19/spied-hyundai-kona-seen-in-malaysia-debut-soon/\">sighted in its current form</a> on roads ahead of a local market debut that will likely take place soon. The compact SUV was previewed at KLIMS18 with the 1.6 litre Gamma T-GDI powertrain with seven-speed dual clutch automatic gearbox, which is the most likely combination that Malaysia will receive. </p>\n<p>This will enter the B-segment SUV field, where the players from Japanese makes include the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/06/29/mazda-cx-3-limited-edition-accessories-package-bodykit-suede-interior-chassis-bracing-jbl-rm14-5k/\">Mazda CX-3</a>, <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/07/21/quick-look-2020-honda-hr-v-rs-brown-interior/\">Honda HR-V</a> and the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/08/06/2020-toyota-c-hr-gets-improved-safety-kit-in-japan/\">Toyota C-HR</a>. The Kona has also been slated to offer a fully electric version that will be offered for our market via leasing through official channels, and will similarly get full aftersales support from the manufacturer, as with its internal combustion siblings. </p>\n<p>The petrol versions will kick off proceedings in Malaysia, and based on the kit list from the 2018 example, this could include a premium sound system by Krell, wireless charging and Hyundai’s full suite of active safety and driver assist systems. Of course, local market specification can only be known for sure once details have been made official.</p>\n<p><strong>GALLERY: 2018 Hyundai Kona 1.6 Turbo</strong></p>\n\n<a 16:54:42","updatedTime":"2020-08-26 16:54:42","title":"Jaguar XE facelift debuts in Malaysia – R-Dynamic 2.0L, 300 PS, RM396k with 50% sales tax exemption","link":"https://paultan.org/?p=1166600","description":"<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/02/27/jaguar-xe-facelift-unveiled-with-updated-styling-tech/2019-jaguar-xe-facelift-1/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-927283\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-1-630x331.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"331\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-927283\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-1-630x331.jpg 630w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-1-1200x630.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-1-850x446.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Jaguar Land Rover Malaysia has introduced the 2020 Jaguar XE in the country, the facelift &#8211; which had its <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/02/27/jaguar-xe-facelift-unveiled-with-updated-styling-tech/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">global reveal in February 2019</a> &#8211; going on sale here in a solitary R-Dynamic guise.</p>\n<p>It&#8217;s powered by a 2.0 litre Ingenium engine in its P300 configuration, which for output offers 300 PS at 5,500 rpm and 400 Nm between 1,500 to 4,500 rpm. Paired with a ZF 8HP45 eight-speed automatic transmission, the rear-wheel drive XE does the 0-100 km/h sprint in 5.9 seconds and has a 250 km/h top speed.</p>\n<p>Exterior changes brought about by the refresh include new, sleeker LED headlights, which continue to feature J-shaped daytime running lights. The car also gets a new front bumper, and on the R-Dynamic it&#8217;s a sportier design with more prominently sculptured inlets compared to the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2016/01/28/jaguar-xe-debuts-in-malaysia/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">pre-facelift</a>, with a U-shaped “wing” adding further emphasis on the width at the front.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://paultan.org/2019/02/27/jaguar-xe-facelift-unveiled-with-updated-styling-tech/2019-jaguar-xe-facelift-10/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-927292\"><img src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-10-630x331.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"630\" height=\"331\" class=\"alignnone size-medium wp-image-927292\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-10-630x331.jpg 630w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-10-1200x630.jpg 1200w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-10-850x446.jpg 850w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 630px) 100vw, 630px\" /></a></p>\n<p>At the rear, there&#8217;s also a new bumper with dual integrated exhausts and new LED tail lights, which feature new graphics. The R-Dynamic version also get dark mesh detailing on the rear valence as well as a number of new 18-inch wheel design choices.</p>\n<p>Inside, the cabin, which is dressed with sports-style seats featuring contrast stitching, satin chrome gearshift paddles and R-Dynamic treadplates, gets a number of redesigned items, such as a steering wheel taken from the <a href=\"https://paultan.org/2020/06/23/2020-jaguar-i-pace-pivi-pro-cockpit-11-kw-charger/\" rel=\"noopener\" target=\"_blank\">I-Pace</a> as well as a new SportShift gear selector and JaguarDrive Control switch.</p>\n<p>The centre console has been given a significant overhaul, and now features a Touch Pro Duo infotainment system with dual high-resolution touchscreens. The upper 10-inch display provides access to infotainment, navigation and media functions, while a 5.5-inch lower unit allows for dual-tasking and climate control accessibility, complete with dynamic rotary dials.</p>\n\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2019/02/27/jaguar-xe-facelift-unveiled-with-updated-styling-tech/2019-jaguar-xe-facelift-44/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-44-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-44-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-44-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-44-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-44-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-44-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n<a href='https://paultan.org/2019/02/27/jaguar-xe-facelift-unveiled-with-updated-styling-tech/2019-jaguar-xe-facelift-41/'><img width=\"108\" height=\"108\" src=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-41-108x108.jpg\" class=\"attachment-thumbnail size-thumbnail\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-41-108x108.jpg 108w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-41-70x70.jpg 70w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-41-80x80.jpg 80w, http://s3.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-41-160x160.jpg 160w, http://s1.paultan.org/image/2019/02/2019-Jaguar-XE-facelift-41-216x216.jpg 216w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 108px) 100vw, 108px\" /></a>\n\n<p>Also to be found is a 12.3-inch digital instrument cluster and an assortment of convenience kit. There&#8217;s  a smartphone pack for Apple CarPlay/Android Auto connectivity as well as wireless charging, and also included in the kit list is Smart Settings, which uses artificial intelligence to learn the preferences of individual drivers and adjusts seat, mirror, audio and climate settings automatically.</p>\n<p>Pricing for the facelifted Jaguar XE R-Dynamic variant starts from RM395,831 (excluding road tax and insurance). The stated price is inclusive of the 50% sales tax waiver provided under the Penjana economic stimulus plan. </p>\n<p>The XE comes with a Jaguar Care programme, which includes a five-year warranty, five-year free service package and three years of roadside assistance.</p>\n<p><strong>GALLERY: Jaguar XE facelift, R-Dynamic variant</strong>\n<a
